Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Authenticating apis

Requests for authenticating

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"mobile\": 9376537379,
    \"password\": \"amin1234\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "mobile": 9376537379,
    "password": "amin1234"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Request      

POST api/v1/login

Body Parameters

mobile   integer   

The mobile of the user. Defaults to 09376537379.

password   string  optional  

The password of the user. Defaults to amin1234.

Endpoints

GET api/v1/ssss

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/v1/ssss" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/ssss"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 58
access-control-allow-origin: *

GET api/v1/ssss

Api to forgot password

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/forgotPassword" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"mobile\": 9376537379,
    \"activation_code\": \"45202\",
    \"password\": \"amin1234\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/forgotPassword"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "mobile": 9376537379,
    "activation_code": "45202",
    "password": "amin1234"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/v1/forgotPassword

Body Parameters

mobile   integer   

The mobile of the user. Defaults to 09376537379.

activation_code   string  optional  

Must be 5 digits.

password   string  optional  

The password of the user. Defaults to amin1234.

GET api/v1/logout

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/v1/logout" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/logout"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

POST /deviceTokens

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/deviceToken/submit" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"device_id\": \"et\",
    \"device_model\": \"cumque\",
    \"firebase_token\": \"aliquid\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/deviceToken/submit"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "device_id": "et",
    "device_model": "cumque",
    "firebase_token": "aliquid"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Mark as read

Returns the list of unread notifications

    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"

    "http://localhost/api/v1/notifications/readall"
);

    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

);

Security section

Apis to set two factor login and cancel it

POST api/v1/security/setTwoFactorLogin

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/security/setTwoFactorLogin" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"mobile\": 93765537379,
    \"login_type\": 1,
    \"activation_code\": 11,
    \"secret_key\": \"explicabo\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/security/setTwoFactorLogin"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "mobile": 93765537379,
    "login_type": 1,
    "activation_code": 11,
    "secret_key": "explicabo"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Request      

POST api/v1/security/setTwoFactorLogin

Body Parameters

mobile   integer  optional  

mobile number of user. Defaults to 093765537379.

login_type   integer  optional  

the number of login type. Defaults to 1.

activation_code   integer  optional  

activation code is 5 digit.

secret_key   string  optional  

secret key.

POST api/v1/security/disableTwoFactorLogin

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/security/disableTwoFactorLogin" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"disable\": true
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/security/disableTwoFactorLogin"
);

Upgrade Level One

Submits a request for user's level one upgrade

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user/upgradeLevelOne" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "first_name=Ali" \
    --form "last_name=moradi" \
    --form "gender=1" \
    --form "birth_date=1377/4/13" \
    --form "national_card_number=3128491052" \
    --form "national_card_image=@C:\Users\alip\AppData\Local\Temp\phpB796.tmp" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user/upgradeLevelOne"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('first_name', 'Ali');
body.append('last_name', 'moradi');
body.append('gender', '1');
body.append('birth_date', '1377/4/13');
body.append('national_card_number', '3128491052');
body.append('national_card_image', document.querySelector('input[name="national_card_image"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "status": 200,
    "message": "ÿØÿ±ÿÆŸàÿßÿ≥ÿ™ ÿßÿ≠ÿ±ÿßÿ≤ ŸáŸà€åÿ™ ÿ≥ÿ∑ÿ≠ €å⁄© ÿ®ÿß ŸÖŸàŸÅŸÇ€åÿ™ ÿ´ÿ®ÿ™ ÿ¥ÿØ",
    "data": null,
    "code": 200
}
Received response:

Manual Withdraw

Submits a withdraw request for the user

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user_wallets/manual_withdraw" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"amount\": 0,
    \"wallet_address\": \"862454896326559844125795442365\",
    \"exchange_symbol\": \"BTC\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user_wallets/manual_withdraw"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "amount": 0,
    "wallet_address": "862454896326559844125795442365",
    "exchange_symbol": "BTC"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Response Fields

data   string   

the code we can find the deposit request with

Manual Deposit

Submits a deposit request for the user

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user_wallets/manual_deposit" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"transaction_code\": \"862454896326559844125795442365\",
    \"exchange_symbol\": \"BTC\",
    \"amount\": 0
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/user_wallets/manual_deposit"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "transaction_code": "862454896326559844125795442365",
    "exchange_symbol": "BTC",
    "amount": 0
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

User financial section

Api to perform operations on cards

Api to create card

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/v1/financial/create" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"title\": \"melal.\",
    \"sheba_number\": \"IR020750023811005124176497.\",
    \"account_number\": 23811005124176496,
    \"cart_number\": 6062561013777266
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/v1/financial/create"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "title": "melal.",
    "sheba_number": "IR020750023811005124176497.",
    "account_number": 23811005124176496,
    "cart_number": 6062561013777266
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
